Navigate to `http://localhost:3033` in your web browser\n2. You\'ll see the Dashboard with an overview of your sandboxes\n\n### Creating Your First Sandbox\n\n1. Click the **"Create Sandbox"** button on the Dashboard\n2. Fill in the sandbox configuration:\n   - **Name**: A descriptive name for your sandbox\n   - **Base Image**: Select a Docker image (Python, Node.js, Ubuntu, etc.)\n   - **GPU Type**: Optional - select if you need GPU acceleration\n   - **Time to Live**: How long the sandbox should run before auto-termination\n3. Click **"Create Sandbox"**\n4. Wait for the sandbox to be created (status will change from "creating" to "running")\n\n---\n\n## Dashboard\n\nThe Dashboard provides an at-a-glance view of your sandbox environment:\n\n### Statistics Cards\n\n- **Total Sandboxes**: Total number of sandboxes you\'ve created\n- **Running**: Number of currently active sandboxes\n- **Stopped**: Number of paused sandboxes\n- **Creating**: Number of sandboxes being initialized\n\n### Recent Sandboxes\n\nView your most recently created sandboxes with:\n- Sandbox name and base image\n- Current status (running, stopped, creating, etc.)\n- GPU type (if applicable)\n- Creation time\n- Time remaining before auto-termination\n- Quick action buttons (Start, Stop, Terminate)\n\n---\n\n## Managing Sandboxes\n\n### Sandbox List\n\nAccess the full list of sandboxes from the sidebar navigation:\n\n1. Click **"Sandboxes"** in the sidebar\n2. Use the search bar to find specific sandboxes\n3. Filter by status using the dropdown menu\n\n### Sandbox Actions\n\n#### Starting a Sandbox\n\n1. Find the stopped sandbox\n2. Click the **"Start"** button\n3. Wait for status to change to "running"\n\n#### Stopping a Sandbox\n\n1. Find the running sandbox\n2. Click the **"Stop"** button\n3. The sandbox will pause but retain its state\n\n#### Terminating a Sandbox\n\n1. Click the **"Terminate"** button\n2. Confirm the action in the dialog\n3. The sandbox and all its data will be permanently deleted\n\n### Sandbox Details\n\nClick on any sandbox card to view detailed information:\n\n- **Status and Configuration**: Current state, image, GPU type\n- **Time Information**: Created time, time remaining\n- **Resource Metrics**: Real-time charts showing resource usage\n- **Quick Actions**: Open code editor, view monitoring, manage files\n\n---\n\n## Code Editor\n\nThe integrated code editor allows you to write and execute code directly in your sandbox.\n\n### Opening the Editor\n\n1. From the Dashboard or Sandbox Details, click **"Open Code Editor"**\n2. Or navigate to **"Code Editor"** in the sidebar\n\n### Writing Code\n\n1. Select your programming language from the dropdown\n2. Write your code in the Monaco editor (same editor as VS Code)\n3. The editor provides:\n   - Syntax highlighting\n   - Auto-completion\n   - Line numbers\n   - Code folding\n\n### Running Code\n\n1. Click the **"Run Code"** button\n2. View output in the right panel\n3. Errors will be displayed in red\n4. Standard output appears in the output panel\n\n### Supported Languages\n\n- Python (3.10, 3.11)\n- JavaScript (Node.js 18, 20)\n- TypeScript\n- Java\n- C++\n- Go\n- Rust\n\n### File Operations\n\n- **Upload**: Click "Upload" to load code from your computer\n- **Save**: Click "Save" to download your code\n- Files are automatically named based on the selected language\n\n---\n\n## Resource Monitoring\n\nMonitor your sandbox\'s resource usage in real-time.\n\n### Available Metrics\n\n#### CPU Usage\n- Real-time CPU utilization percentage\n- Historical data shown in line chart\n- Helps identify CPU-intensive operations\n\n#### Memory Usage\n- Current memory consumption in MB and percentage\n- Memory trends over time\n- Useful for detecting memory leaks\n\n#### GPU Utilization (if available)\n- GPU usage percentage\n- GPU memory consumption\n- Only available for sandboxes with GPU support\n\n#### Disk I/O\n- Disk read operations (MB)\n- Disk write operations (MB)\n- Helps identify I/O bottlenecks\n\n#### Network Traffic\n- Network received (MB)\n- Network transmitted (MB)\n- Monitor data transfer rates\n\n### Accessing Monitoring\n\n1. Navigate to sandbox details\n2. Scroll down to the "Resource Metrics" section\n3. View real-time charts for all metrics\n4. Or click **"View Monitoring"** for full-screen view\n\n---\n\n## File Management\n\nManage files within your sandbox environment.\n\n### Uploading Files\n\n1. Navigate to **"Files"** in the sidebar\n2. Select your sandbox\n3. Click **"Upload"** button\n4. Choose files from your computer\n5. Files are uploaded to the sandbox filesystem\n\n### Downloading Files\n\n1. Browse the file tree\n2. Select the file you want to download\n3. Click the **"Download"** button\n4. File will be saved to your computer\n\n### File Operations\n\n- **Create**: Create new files or directories\n- **Delete**: Remove files or directories\n- **Rename**: Change file or directory names\n- **Navigate**: Browse through the directory structure\n\n### Snapshots\n\nSave the current state of your sandbox:\n\n1. Click **"Create Snapshot"**\n2. Enter a name and description\n3. The snapshot is saved\n4. Restore later by clicking **"Restore"** on the snapshot\n\n---\n\n## Testing\n\nRun automated tests for iTechSmart products within sandboxes.\n\n### Running Tests\n\n1. Navigate to **"Tests"** in the sidebar\n2. Select your sandbox\n3. Choose the product to test\n4. Select test type\n5. Click **"Run Test"**\n\n### Test Types\n\n- **Unit Tests**: Test individual components\n- **Integration Tests**: Test component interactions\n- **End-to-End Tests**: Test complete workflows\n- **Performance Tests**: Measure performance metrics\n\n### Viewing Results\n\n- Test status (pending, running, passed, failed)\n- Detailed results and logs\n- Error messages for failed tests\n- Test history and trends\n\n---\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### Resource Management\n\n1. **Set Appropriate TTL**: Choose a time-to-live that matches your needs\n2. **Stop Unused Sandboxes**: Stop sandboxes when not in use to save resources\n3. **Monitor Resource Usage**: Keep an eye on CPU, memory, and disk usage\n4. **Clean Up**: Terminate sandboxes you no longer need\n\n### Security\n\n1. **Don\'t Store Sensitive Data**: Sandboxes are temporary environments\n2. **Use Snapshots**: Save important work before termination\n3. **Review Code**: Always review code before execution\n4. **Limit Permissions**: Use appropriate base images with minimal permissions\n\n### Performance\n\n1. **Choose Right Image**: Select the most appropriate base image\n2. **Use GPU When Needed**: Enable GPU for ML/AI workloads\n3. **Optimize Code**: Write efficient code to minimize resource usage\n4. **Monitor Metrics**: Use monitoring to identify bottlenecks\n\n### Development Workflow\n\n1. **Create Template**: Save common configurations as templates\n2. **Use Snapshots**: Create snapshots at key milestones\n3. **Test Incrementally**: Test code changes in small increments\n4. **Document Work**: Keep notes on sandbox configurations\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Sandbox Won\'t Start\n\n**Problem**: Sandbox stuck in "creating" status\n\n**Solutions**:\n1. Wait a few minutes - creation can take time\n2. Check if the base image is valid\n3. Verify sufficient system resources\n4. Try terminating and recreating\n\n### Code Execution Fails\n\n**Problem**: Code doesn\'t run or produces errors\n\n**Solutions**:\n1. Check syntax errors in your code\n2. Verify the correct language is selected\n3. Ensure required dependencies are installed\n4. Check sandbox logs for detailed errors\n\n### High Resource Usage\n\n**Problem**: Sandbox consuming too many resources\n\n**Solutions**:\n1. Review your code for inefficiencies\n2. Check for infinite loops or memory leaks\n3. Consider using a more powerful base image\n4. Enable GPU if running ML/AI workloads\n\n### Connection Issues\n\n**Problem**: Can\'t connect to sandbox or API\n\n**Solutions**:\n1. Check your internet connection\n2. Verify the backend is running\n3. Check firewall settings\n4. Try refreshing the page\n\n### File Upload Fails\n\n**Problem**: Can\'t upload files to sandbox\n\n**Solutions**:\n1. Check file size (must be under limit)\n2. Verify sandbox is running\n3. Ensure sufficient disk space\n4. Try uploading smaller files\n\n### Snapshot Restore Fails\n\n**Problem**: Can\'t restore from snapshot\n\n**Solutions**:\n1. Verify snapshot exists and is valid\n2. Check if sandbox is stopped\n3. Ensure sufficient resources\n4. Try creating a new sandbox from snapshot\n\n---\n\n## Getting Help\n\nIf you encounter issues not covered in this guide:\n\n1. Check the [API Documentation](./API.md)\n2. Review the [Architecture Guide](./ARCHITECTURE.md)\n3. Contact iTechSmart Inc. support\n4. Visit our documentation portal\n\n---\n\n## Appendix\n\n### Keyboard Shortcuts (Code Editor)\n\n- `Ctrl/Cmd + S`: Save code\n- `Ctrl/Cmd + Enter`: Run code\n- `Ctrl/Cmd + /`: Toggle comment\n- `Ctrl/Cmd + F`: Find\n- `Ctrl/Cmd + H`: Replace\n\n### Common Base Images\n\n- `python:3.11`: Python 3.11 with pip\n- `python:3.10`: Python 3.10 with pip\n- `node:20`: Node.js 20 with npm\n- `node:18`: Node.js 18 with npm\n- `ubuntu:22.04`: Ubuntu 22.04 LTS\n- `ubuntu:20.04`: Ubuntu 20.04 LTS\n\n### GPU Types\n\n- **T4**: NVIDIA Tesla T4 (16GB, good for inference)\n- **A10G**: NVIDIA A10G (24GB, balanced performance)\n- **V100**: NVIDIA V100 (16GB/32GB, high performance)\n- **A100**: NVIDIA A100 (40GB/80GB, top performance)\n\n---\n\n**Last Updated**: August 8, 2025  \n**Version**: 1.0.0  \n**Copyright**: ¬© 2025 iTechSmart Inc.. [Overview](#overview)\n2. [Prerequisites](#prerequisites)\n3. [Local Development](#local-development)\n4. [Docker Deployment](#docker-deployment)\n5. [Production Deployment](#production-deployment)\n6. [Configuration](#configuration)\n7. [Monitoring](#monitoring)\n8. [Backup & Recovery](#backup--recovery)\n9. [Scaling](#scaling)\n10. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\nThis guide covers deploying iTechSmart Sandbox in various environments, from local development to production.\n\n### Architecture Components\n\n- **Frontend**: React + TypeScript (Port 3033)\n- **Backend**: FastAPI + Python (Port 8033)\n- **Database**: PostgreSQL 15\n- **Cache**: Redis 7\n- **Container Runtime**: Docker\n\n---\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n### System Requirements\n\n#### Minimum Requirements\n- **CPU**: 4 cores\n- **RAM**: 8 GB\n- **Disk**: 50 GB SSD\n- **OS**: Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+, Debian 11+, CentOS 8+)\n\n#### Recommended Requirements\n- **CPU**: 8+ cores\n- **RAM**: 16+ GB\n- **Disk**: 100+ GB SSD\n- **OS**: Ubuntu 22.04 LTS\n- **GPU**: Optional (NVIDIA with CUDA support)\n\n### Software Requirements\n\n- Docker 24.0+\n- Docker Compose 2.20+\n- Git 2.30+\n- Node.js 20+ (for local development)\n- Python 3.11+ (for local development)\n\n### Network Requirements\n\n- Ports 3033 (frontend), 8033 (backend) available\n- Internet access for pulling Docker images\n- Firewall configured to allow required ports\n\n---\n\n## Local Development\n\n### Backend Setup\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to backend directory\ncd itechsmart-sandbox/backend\n\n# Create virtual environment\npython -m venv venv\nsource venv/bin/activate  # On Windows: venv\\Scripts\\activate\n\n# Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Set up environment variables\ncp .env.example .env\n# Edit .env with your configuration\n\n# Run database migrations\nalembic upgrade head\n\n# Start the backend server\nuvicorn main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8033 --reload\n```\n\n### Frontend Setup\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to frontend directory\ncd itechsmart-sandbox/frontend\n\n# Install dependencies\nnpm install\n\n# Set up environment variables\ncp .env.example .env\n# Edit .env with your configuration\n\n# Start the development server\nnpm run dev\n```\n\n### Database Setup\n\n```bash\n# Start PostgreSQL with Docker\ndocker run -d \\\n  --name sandbox-postgres \\\n  -e POSTGRES_USER=sandbox_user \\\n  -e POSTGRES_PASSWORD=sandbox_pass \\\n  -e POSTGRES_DB=sandbox_db \\\n  -p 5432:5432 \\\n  postgres:15-alpine\n\n# Start Redis with Docker\ndocker run -d \\\n  --name sandbox-redis \\\n  -p 6379:6379 \\\n  redis:7-alpine\n```\n\n---\n\n## Docker Deployment\n\n### Using Docker Compose (Recommended)\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to project root\ncd itechsmart-sandbox\n\n# Build and start all services\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n# View logs\ndocker-compose logs -f\n\n# Stop all services\ndocker-compose down\n\n# Stop and remove volumes (WARNING: deletes data)\ndocker-compose down -v\n```\n\n### Individual Container Deployment\n\n#### Backend\n\n```bash\ncd itechsmart-sandbox/backend\n\n# Build image\ndocker build -t itechsmart-sandbox-backend .\n\n# Run container\ndocker run -d \\\n  --name sandbox-backend \\\n  -p 8033:8033 \\\n  -e DATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:pass@host:5432/db \\\n  -e REDIS_URL=redis://host:6379 \\\n  -v /var/run/docker.sock:/var/run/docker.sock \\\n  itechsmart-sandbox-backend\n```\n\n#### Frontend\n\n```bash\ncd itechsmart-sandbox/frontend\n\n# Build image\ndocker build -t itechsmart-sandbox-frontend .\n\n# Run container\ndocker run -d \\\n  --name sandbox-frontend \\\n  -p 3033:3033 \\\n  -e VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:8033 \\\n  itechsmart-sandbox-frontend\n```\n\n---\n\n## Production Deployment\n\n### Pre-Deployment Checklist\n\n- [ ] Update all environment variables\n- [ ] Configure SSL/TLS certificates\n- [ ] Set up database backups\n- [ ] Configure monitoring and logging\n- [ ] Review security settings\n- [ ] Test disaster recovery procedures\n- [ ] Document deployment process\n\n### Environment Variables\n\nCreate a `.env.production` file:\n\n```env\n# Backend Configuration\nDATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:password@db-host:5432/sandbox_db\nREDIS_URL=redis://redis-host:6379\nSECRET_KEY=your-super-secret-key-change-this\nENVIRONMENT=production\nDEBUG=false\n\n# Security\nALLOWED_HOSTS=yourdomain.com,www.yourdomain.com\nCORS_ORIGINS=https://yourdomain.com\n\n# Docker Configuration\nDOCKER_HOST=unix:///var/run/docker.sock\nMAX_SANDBOXES=100\nDEFAULT_TTL=3600\n\n# Frontend Configuration\nVITE_API_URL=https://api.yourdomain.com\nVITE_ENV=production\n```\n\n### SSL/TLS Configuration\n\n#### Using Nginx as Reverse Proxy\n\n```nginx\n# /etc/nginx/sites-available/sandbox\n\nserver {\n    listen 80;\n    server_name yourdomain.com;\n    return 301 https://$server_name$request_uri;\n}\n\nserver {\n    listen 443 ssl http2;\n    server_name yourdomain.com;\n\n    ssl_certificate /etc/ssl/certs/yourdomain.com.crt;\n    ssl_certificate_key /etc/ssl/private/yourdomain.com.key;\n    ssl_protocols TLSv1.2 TLSv1.3;\n    ssl_ciphers HIGH:!aNULL:!MD5;\n\n    # Frontend\n    location / {\n        proxy_pass http://localhost:3033;\n        proxy_http_version 1.1;\n        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;\n        proxy_set_header Connection \'upgrade\';\n        proxy_set_header Host $host;\n        proxy_cache_bypass $http_upgrade;\n    }\n\n    # Backend API\n    location /api {\n        proxy_pass http://localhost:8033;\n        proxy_http_version 1.1;\n        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;\n        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;\n        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Database Configuration\n\n#### PostgreSQL Production Settings\n\n```sql\n-- Create production database\nCREATE DATABASE sandbox_db;\nCREATE USER sandbox_user WITH ENCRYPTED PASSWORD \'strong-password\';\nGRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON DATABASE sandbox_db TO sandbox_user;\n\n-- Performance tuning\nALTER SYSTEM SET shared_buffers = \'4GB\';\nALTER SYSTEM SET effective_cache_size = \'12GB\';\nALTER SYSTEM SET maintenance_work_mem = \'1GB\';\nALTER SYSTEM SET checkpoint_completion_target = 0.9;\nALTER SYSTEM SET wal_buffers = \'16MB\';\nALTER SYSTEM SET default_statistics_target = 100;\nALTER SYSTEM SET random_page_cost = 1.1;\nALTER SYSTEM SET effective_io_concurrency = 200;\nALTER SYSTEM SET work_mem = \'10MB\';\nALTER SYSTEM SET min_wal_size = \'1GB\';\nALTER SYSTEM SET max_wal_size = \'4GB\';\n\n-- Restart PostgreSQL\nSELECT pg_reload_conf();\n```\n\n### Systemd Service Files\n\n#### Backend Service\n\n```ini\n# /etc/systemd/system/sandbox-backend.service\n\n[Unit]\nDescription=iTechSmart Sandbox Backend\nAfter=network.target postgresql.service redis.service\n\n[Service]\nType=simple\nUser=sandbox\nWorkingDirectory=/opt/itechsmart-sandbox/backend\nEnvironment="PATH=/opt/itechsmart-sandbox/backend/venv/bin"\nExecStart=/opt/itechsmart-sandbox/backend/venv/bin/uvicorn main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8033\nRestart=always\nRestartSec=10\n\n[Install]\nWantedBy=multi-user.target\n```\n\n#### Frontend Service\n\n```ini\n# /etc/systemd/system/sandbox-frontend.service\n\n[Unit]\nDescription=iTechSmart Sandbox Frontend\nAfter=network.target\n\n[Service]\nType=simple\nUser=sandbox\nWorkingDirectory=/opt/itechsmart-sandbox/frontend\nExecStart=/usr/bin/npm run preview -- --port 3033 --host 0.0.0.0\nRestart=always\nRestartSec=10\n\n[Install]\nWantedBy=multi-user.target\n```\n\nEnable and start services:\n\n```bash\nsudo systemctl enable sandbox-backend sandbox-frontend\nsudo systemctl start sandbox-backend sandbox-frontend\nsudo systemctl status sandbox-backend sandbox-frontend\n```\n\n---\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Backend Configuration\n\nKey configuration files:\n- `backend/config.py`: Application settings\n- `backend/database.py`: Database connection\n- `backend/.env`: Environment variables\n\n### Frontend Configuration\n\nKey configuration files:\n- `frontend/vite.config.ts`: Build configuration\n- `frontend/nginx.conf`: Nginx settings\n- `frontend/.env`: Environment variables\n\n### Docker Configuration\n\nKey configuration files:\n- `docker-compose.yml`: Multi-container setup\n- `backend/Dockerfile`: Backend image\n- `frontend/Dockerfile`: Frontend image\n\n---\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Health Checks\n\n```bash\n# Backend health check\ncurl http://localhost:8033/health\n\n# Frontend health check\ncurl http://localhost:3033/\n\n# Database health check\ndocker exec sandbox-postgres pg_isready\n```\n\n### Logging\n\n#### Backend Logs\n\n```bash\n# Docker logs\ndocker logs -f sandbox-backend\n\n# Systemd logs\nsudo journalctl -u sandbox-backend -f\n```\n\n#### Frontend Logs\n\n```bash\n# Docker logs\ndocker logs -f sandbox-frontend\n\n# Systemd logs\nsudo journalctl -u sandbox-frontend -f\n```\n\n### Metrics Collection\n\nRecommended tools:\n- **Prometheus**: Metrics collection\n- **Grafana**: Visualization\n- **ELK Stack**: Log aggregation\n- **Sentry**: Error tracking\n\n---\n\n## Backup & Recovery\n\n### Database Backup\n\n```bash\n# Create backup\ndocker exec sandbox-postgres pg_dump -U sandbox_user sandbox_db > backup_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).sql\n\n# Restore backup\ndocker exec -i sandbox-postgres psql -U sandbox_user sandbox_db < backup.sql\n```\n\n### Automated Backups\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# /opt/scripts/backup-sandbox.sh\n\nBACKUP_DIR="/opt/backups/sandbox"\nDATE=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)\n\n# Create backup directory\nmkdir -p $BACKUP_DIR\n\n# Backup database\ndocker exec sandbox-postgres pg_dump -U sandbox_user sandbox_db | gzip > $BACKUP_DIR/db_$DATE.sql.gz\n\n# Backup Redis\ndocker exec sandbox-redis redis-cli SAVE\ndocker cp sandbox-redis:/data/dump.rdb $BACKUP_DIR/redis_$DATE.rdb\n\n# Remove old backups (keep last 7 days)\nfind $BACKUP_DIR -name "*.sql.gz" -mtime +7 -delete\nfind $BACKUP_DIR -name "*.rdb" -mtime +7 -delete\n\necho "Backup completed: $DATE"\n```\n\nAdd to crontab:\n\n```bash\n# Run daily at 2 AM\n0 2 * * * /opt/scripts/backup-sandbox.sh\n```\n\n---\n\n## Scaling\n\n### Horizontal Scaling\n\n#### Backend Scaling\n\n```yaml\n# docker-compose.yml\nservices:\n  backend:\n    deploy:\n      replicas: 3\n      resources:\n        limits:\n          cpus: \'2\'\n          memory: 4G\n```\n\n#### Load Balancer Configuration\n\n```nginx\nupstream backend {\n    least_conn;\n    server backend1:8033;\n    server backend2:8033;\n    server backend3:8033;\n}\n\nserver {\n    location /api {\n        proxy_pass http://backend;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Vertical Scaling\n\nIncrease resources in docker-compose.yml:\n\n```yaml\nservices:\n  backend:\n    deploy:\n      resources:\n        limits:\n          cpus: \'4\'\n          memory: 8G\n        reservations:\n          cpus: \'2\'\n          memory: 4G\n```\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### Port Already in Use\n\n```bash\n# Find process using port\nsudo lsof -i :8033\nsudo lsof -i :3033\n\n# Kill process\nsudo kill -9 <PID>\n```\n\n#### Database Connection Failed\n\n```bash\n# Check PostgreSQL status\ndocker exec sandbox-postgres pg_isready\n\n# Check connection\npsql -h localhost -U sandbox_user -d sandbox_db\n```\n\n#### Docker Socket Permission Denied\n\n```bash\n# Add user to docker group\nsudo usermod -aG docker $USER\n\n# Restart session\nnewgrp docker\n```\n\n#### Out of Disk Space\n\n```bash\n# Check disk usage\ndf -h\n\n# Clean Docker\ndocker system prune -a --volumes\n\n# Remove old images\ndocker image prune -a\n```\n\n---\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n### Best Practices\n\n1. **Use Strong Passwords**: Generate secure passwords for all services\n2. **Enable SSL/TLS**: Always use HTTPS in production\n3. **Regular Updates**: Keep all dependencies up to date\n4. **Firewall Rules**: Restrict access to necessary ports only\n5. **Backup Encryption**: Encrypt backup files\n6. **Access Control**: Implement proper authentication and authorization\n7. **Audit Logs**: Enable and monitor audit logs\n8. **Security Scanning**: Regularly scan for vulnerabilities\n\n### Firewall Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Allow SSH\nsudo ufw allow 22/tcp\n\n# Allow HTTP/HTTPS\nsudo ufw allow 80/tcp\nsudo ufw allow 443/tcp\n\n# Allow backend (if needed externally)\nsudo ufw allow 8033/tcp\n\n# Enable firewall\nsudo ufw enable\n```\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\nFor deployment assistance:\n- Email: support@itechsmart.ai\n- Documentation: https://docs.itechsmart.ai\n- GitHub Issues: https://github.com/itechsmart/sandbox/issues\n\n---\n\n**Last Updated**: August 8, 2025  \n**Version**: 1.0.0  \n**Copyright**: ¬© 2025 iTechSmart Inc.. {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="infrastructure/terraform/aws/README.md">\n# iTechSmart Suite - AWS Terraform Infrastructure\n\nThis directory contains Terraform configurations for deploying the iTechSmart Suite to AWS.\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\nThe infrastructure includes:\n- **VPC** with public and private subnets across 3 availability zones\n- **Application Load Balancer** for traffic distribution\n- **ECS Fargate** cluster for containerized applications\n- **RDS PostgreSQL** for database\n- **ElastiCache Redis** for caching\n- **ECR** repositories for Docker images\n- **S3** buckets for application data\n- **CloudWatch** for logging and monitoring\n- **IAM** roles and policies for security\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n1. **AWS Account** with appropriate permissions\n2. **Terraform** >= 1.0 installed\n3. **AWS CLI** configured with credentials\n4. **S3 Bucket** for Terraform state (create manually first)\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### 1. Configure AWS Credentials\n\n```bash\naws configure\n```\n\n### 2. Create S3 Bucket for Terraform State\n\n```bash\naws s3 mb s3://itechsmart-terraform-state --region us-east-1\naws s3api put-bucket-versioning \\\n  --bucket itechsmart-terraform-state \\\n  --versioning-configuration Status=Enabled\n```\n\n### 3. Initialize Terraform\n\n```bash\ncd infrastructure/terraform/aws\nterraform init\n```\n\n### 4. Configure Variables\n\n```bash\ncp terraform.tfvars.example terraform.tfvars\n# Edit terraform.tfvars with your values\nvim terraform.tfvars\n```\n\n### 5. Plan Deployment\n\n```bash\nterraform plan\n```\n\n### 6. Deploy Infrastructure\n\n```bash\nterraform apply\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Required Variables\n\n- `db_password` - Database master password (sensitive)\n\n### Optional Variables\n\n- `aws_region` - AWS region (default: us-east-1)\n- `environment` - Environment name (default: production)\n- `vpc_cidr` - VPC CIDR block (default: 10.0.0.0/16)\n- `db_instance_class` - RDS instance type (default: db.t3.large)\n- `redis_node_type` - Redis node type (default: cache.t3.medium)\n\nSee `variables.tf` for all available options.\n\n## Environments\n\n### Development\n```bash\nterraform workspace new development\nterraform workspace select development\nterraform apply -var="environment=development"\n```\n\n### Staging\n```bash\nterraform workspace new staging\nterraform workspace select staging\nterraform apply -var="environment=staging"\n```\n\n### Production\n```bash\nterraform workspace new production\nterraform workspace select production\nterraform apply -var="environment=production"\n```\n\n## Outputs\n\nAfter deployment, Terraform provides:\n- `vpc_id` - VPC identifier\n- `alb_dns_name` - Load balancer DNS name\n- `ecs_cluster_name` - ECS cluster name\n- `rds_endpoint` - Database endpoint\n- `redis_endpoint` - Redis endpoint\n- `ecr_repositories` - Docker registry URLs\n- `s3_bucket_name` - Application data bucket\n\n## Cost Estimation\n\n### Development Environment (~$200/month)\n- ECS Fargate: ~$50\n- RDS db.t3.medium: ~$60\n- ElastiCache cache.t3.micro: ~$15\n- ALB: ~$20\n- Data transfer: ~$20\n- Other services: ~$35\n\n### Production Environment (~$800/month)\n- ECS Fargate: ~$300\n- RDS db.t3.large (Multi-AZ): ~$250\n- ElastiCache cache.t3.medium: ~$80\n- ALB: ~$40\n- Data transfer: ~$80\n- Other services: ~$50\n\n## Security\n\n### Best Practices Implemented\n- ‚úÖ VPC with private subnets for databases\n- ‚úÖ Security groups with least privilege\n- ‚úÖ Encrypted RDS storage\n- ‚úÖ Encrypted S3 buckets\n- ‚úÖ IAM roles with minimal permissions\n- ‚úÖ CloudWatch logging enabled\n- ‚úÖ Multi-AZ deployment for production\n- ‚úÖ Automated backups\n\n### Additional Recommendations\n1. Enable AWS GuardDuty for threat detection\n2. Use AWS Secrets Manager for sensitive data\n3. Enable AWS Config for compliance monitoring\n4. Set up AWS CloudTrail for audit logging\n5. Implement AWS WAF for web application firewall\n\n## Maintenance\n\n### Updating Infrastructure\n\n```bash\n# Pull latest changes\ngit pull\n\n# Review changes\nterraform plan\n\n# Apply updates\nterraform apply\n```\n\n### Backing Up State\n\n```bash\n# State is automatically backed up to S3\n# To manually backup:\nterraform state pull > terraform.tfstate.backup\n```\n\n### Destroying Infrastructure\n\n```bash\n# WARNING: This will destroy all resources\nterraform destroy\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**Issue: Terraform state locked**\n```bash\n# Force unlock (use with caution)\nterraform force-unlock <LOCK_ID>\n```\n\n**Issue: Resource already exists**\n```bash\n# Import existing resource\nterraform import aws_vpc.main vpc-xxxxx\n```\n\n**Issue: Insufficient permissions**\n- Ensure IAM user has required permissions\n- Check AWS CLI credentials: `aws sts get-caller-identity`\n\n### Getting Help\n\n- Check Terraform logs: `TF_LOG=DEBUG terraform apply`\n- Review AWS CloudWatch logs\n- Contact iTechSmart support\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### CloudWatch Dashboards\n\nAccess CloudWatch dashboards for:\n- ECS cluster metrics\n- RDS performance\n- Redis cache hits/misses\n- ALB request metrics\n- Application logs\n\n### Alarms\n\nSet up CloudWatch alarms for:\n- High CPU usage\n- Low memory\n- Database connections\n- Error rates\n- Response times\n\n## Compliance\n\n### HIPAA Compliance\n\nThis infrastructure is designed with HIPAA compliance in mind:\n- ‚úÖ Encrypted data at rest\n- ‚úÖ Encrypted data in transit\n- ‚úÖ Audit logging enabled\n- ‚úÖ Access controls implemented\n- ‚úÖ Backup and recovery procedures\n\n### Additional Steps Required\n1. Sign AWS Business Associate Agreement (BAA)\n2. Enable AWS CloudTrail\n3. Configure AWS Config rules\n4. Implement data retention policies\n5. Install Ansible\n\n**Ubuntu/Debian:**\n```bash\nsudo apt update\nsudo apt install ansible\n```\n\n**macOS:**\n```bash\nbrew install ansible\n```\n\n**Python pip:**\n```bash\npip install ansible\n```\n\n### 2. Clone Repository\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/itechsmart/suite.git\ncd suite/infrastructure/ansible\n```\n\n### 3. Install Required Collections\n\n```bash\nansible-galaxy collection install community.docker\nansible-galaxy collection install community.postgresql\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### 1. Configure Inventory\n\nEdit `inventory/hosts.ini` with your server details:\n\n```ini\n[itechsmart_servers]\nprod-server-1 ansible_host=YOUR_SERVER_IP ansible_user=ubuntu\n```\n\n### 2. Configure Variables\n\nEdit environment-specific variables in `vars/`:\n- `vars/production.yml` - Production settings\n- `vars/staging.yml` - Staging settings\n- `vars/development.yml` - Development settings\n\n### 3. Set Secrets\n\nCreate an Ansible Vault for sensitive data:\n\n```bash\nansible-vault create vars/vault.yml\n```\n\nAdd your secrets:\n```yaml\nvault_database_password: "your-secure-password"\nvault_redis_password: "your-secure-password"\nvault_secret_key: "your-secret-key"\n```\n\n## Deployment\n\n### Quick Start\n\nDeploy to production:\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --extra-vars "environment=production" \\\n  --ask-vault-pass\n```\n\n### Step-by-Step Deployment\n\n#### 1. Test Connection\n```bash\nansible -i inventory/hosts.ini all -m ping\n```\n\n#### 2. Check Playbook Syntax\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml --syntax-check\n```\n\n#### 3. Dry Run\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml --check\n```\n\n#### 4. Deploy\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --extra-vars "environment=production" \\\n  --ask-vault-pass\n```\n\n### Environment-Specific Deployments\n\n**Development:**\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --extra-vars "environment=development" \\\n  --limit itechsmart_dev\n```\n\n**Staging:**\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --extra-vars "environment=staging" \\\n  --limit itechsmart_staging\n```\n\n**Production:**\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --extra-vars "environment=production" \\\n  --limit itechsmart_servers\n```\n\n## This file\n```\n\n## Common Tasks\n\n### Deploy Single Product\n\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --tags "product-deploy" \\\n  --extra-vars "product_name=enterprise"\n```\n\n### Update All Products\n\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --tags "update" \\\n  --extra-vars "itechsmart_version=1.1.0"\n```\n\n### Restart Services\n\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --tags "restart"\n```\n\n### Run Health Checks\n\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --tags "health-check"\n```\n\n### Backup Database\n\n```bash\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml \\\n  --tags "backup"\n```\n\n## Tags\n\nAvailable tags for selective execution:\n- `system-prep` - System preparation only\n- `docker` - Docker installation only\n- `database` - Database deployment only\n- `redis` - Redis deployment only\n- `products` - Products deployment only\n- `monitoring` - Monitoring setup only\n- `backup` - Backup configuration only\n- `health-check` - Health checks only\n- `update` - Update products\n- `restart` - Restart services\n\n## Variables\n\n### Required Variables\n- `environment` - Environment name (production/staging/development)\n- `vault_database_password` - Database password (in vault)\n- `vault_redis_password` - Redis password (in vault)\n\n### Optional Variables\n- `itechsmart_version` - Version to deploy (default: 1.0.0)\n- `itechsmart_base_dir` - Installation directory (default: /opt/itechsmart)\n- `docker_registry` - Docker registry URL\n- `enable_monitoring` - Enable monitoring (default: true)\n- `enable_backup` - Enable backups (default: true)\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Issues\n\n**Problem:** Cannot connect to servers\n```bash\n# Test SSH connection\nssh -i ~/.ssh/key.pem user@server\n\n# Verify inventory\nansible-inventory -i inventory/hosts.ini --list\n```\n\n### Permission Issues\n\n**Problem:** Permission denied\n```bash\n# Use sudo\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml --become --ask-become-pass\n```\n\n### Docker Issues\n\n**Problem:** Docker not starting\n```bash\n# Check Docker status on target\nansible -i inventory/hosts.ini all -m shell -a "systemctl status docker"\n\n# Restart Docker\nansible -i inventory/hosts.ini all -m shell -a "systemctl restart docker" --become\n```\n\n### Deployment Failures\n\n**Problem:** Deployment fails\n```bash\n# Run with verbose output\nansible-playbook -i inventory/hosts.ini playbook.yml -vvv\n\n# Check logs on target\nansible -i inventory/hosts.ini all -m shell -a "docker logs itechsmart-enterprise"\n```\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### Security\n1. Always use Ansible Vault for sensitive data\n2. Use SSH keys instead of passwords\n3. Limit SSH access by IP\n4. Enable firewall on all servers\n5. Regularly update systems and packages\n\n### Performance\n1. Use pipelining for faster execution\n2. Enable fact caching\n3. Use async tasks for long-running operations\n4. Limit parallelism based on resources\n\n### Maintenance\n1. Keep playbooks in version control\n2. Test changes in development first\n3. Document custom modifications\n4. Maintain separate inventories per environment\n5. Regular backup of Ansible vault\n\n## Advanced Usage\n\n### Custom Roles\n\nCreate custom roles for specific needs:\n```bash\nansible-galaxy init roles/custom-role\n```\n\n### Dynamic Inventory\n\nUse dynamic inventory for cloud providers:\n```bash\n# AWS\nansible-playbook -i aws_ec2.yml playbook.yml\n\n# Azure\nansible-playbook -i azure_rm.yml playbook.yml\n```\n\n### Ansible Tower/AWX\n\nFor enterprise deployments, consider using Ansible Tower or AWX for:\n- Web-based UI\n- Role-based access control\n- Job scheduling\n- Audit logging\n- REST API\n\n## Monitoring\n\nAfter deployment, access monitoring dashboards:\n- Prometheus: http://your-server:9090\n- Grafana: http://your-server:3000\n- Enterprise Hub: https://your-server:3001\n\n## Support\n\nFor issues or questions:\n- Email: support@itechsmart.ai\n- Documentation: https://docs.itechsmart.ai\n- GitHub: https://github.com/itechsmart/suite\n\n## Contributing\n\n1. Small to medium deployments, development, testing\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to suite directory\ncd itechsmart-suite\n\n# Start all services\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n# Monitor startup\ndocker-compose logs -f\n```\n\n**Advantages:**\n- ‚úÖ Simplest installation\n- ‚úÖ All services on one server\n- ‚úÖ Easy to manage\n- ‚úÖ Quick setup\n\n#### Method 2: Kubernetes (Recommended for Production)\n\n**Best for:** Large deployments, high availability, auto-scaling\n\n```bash\n# Apply Kubernetes manifests\nkubectl apply -f k8s/\n\n# Check deployment status\nkubectl get pods -n itechsmart\n\n# Access services\nkubectl get services -n itechsmart\n```\n\n**Advantages:**\n- ‚úÖ High availability\n- ‚úÖ Auto-scaling\n- ‚úÖ Load balancing\n- ‚úÖ Self-healing\n\n#### Method 3: Cloud Deployment (Terraform)\n\n**Best for:** Cloud-native deployments, managed services\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to Terraform directory\ncd infrastructure/terraform/aws\n\n# Initialize Terraform\nterraform init\n\n# Deploy infrastructure\nterraform apply\n```\n\n**Advantages:**\n- ‚úÖ Managed services\n- ‚úÖ Automated backups\n- ‚úÖ Built-in monitoring\n- ‚úÖ Global distribution\n\n### Step-by-Step System Preparation**\n\n```bash\n# Update system packages\nsudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade -y\n\n# Install required dependencies\nsudo apt install -y curl wget git vim\n\n# Configure system limits\nsudo sysctl -w vm.max_map_count=262144\nsudo sysctl -w fs.file-max=2097152\n```\n\n**Step 2: Install Docker**\n\n```bash\n# Install Docker\ncurl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh\n\n# Add user to docker group\nsudo usermod -aG docker $USER\n\n# Start Docker service\nsudo systemctl enable docker\nsudo systemctl start docker\n```\n\n**Step 3: Download iTechSmart Suite**\n\n```bash\n# Clone repository\ngit clone https://github.com/itechsmart/suite.git\ncd suite\n\n# Or download release package\nwget https://releases.itechsmart.ai/suite-v1.0.0.tar.gz\ntar -xzf suite-v1.0.0.tar.gz\ncd itechsmart-suite\n```\n\n**Step 4: Configure Environment**\n\n```bash\n# Copy environment template\ncp .env.example .env\n\n# Edit configuration\nnano .env\n```\n\n**Required Configuration:**\n```env\n# Database Configuration\nDATABASE_HOST=localhost\nDATABASE_PORT=5432\nDATABASE_NAME=itechsmart\nDATABASE_USER=itechsmart_admin\nDATABASE_PASSWORD=CHANGE_THIS_PASSWORD\n\n# Redis Configuration\nREDIS_HOST=localhost\nREDIS_PORT=6379\nREDIS_PASSWORD=CHANGE_THIS_PASSWORD\n\n# Security\nSECRET_KEY=GENERATE_RANDOM_SECRET_KEY\nJWT_SECRET=GENERATE_RANDOM_JWT_SECRET\n\n# Domain Configuration\nDOMAIN=your-domain.com\nENABLE_SSL=true\n```\n\n**Step 5: Initialize Database**\n\n```bash\n# Start database container\ndocker-compose up -d postgres\n\n# Wait for database to be ready\nsleep 10\n\n# Run migrations\ndocker-compose run --rm enterprise-backend alembic upgrade head\n```\n\n**Step 6: Deploy Services**\n\n```bash\n# Start all services\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n# Monitor startup logs\ndocker-compose logs -f\n```\n\n**Step 7: Verify Installation**\n\n```bash\n# Check service health\ncurl http://localhost:8001/health\n\n# Check all services\nfor port in {8001..8033}; do\n  echo "Checking port $port..."\n  curl -s http://localhost:$port/health || echo "Service on port $port not ready"\ndone\n```\n\n**Step 8: Access Web Interface**\n\n1. Open browser: `https://your-domain.com:3001`\n2. Accept SSL certificate (if self-signed)\n3. Complete setup wizard\n4. Create administrator account\n5. Configure initial settings\n\n### Post-Installation Configuration\n\n#### Configure SSL/TLS\n\n```bash\n# Install certbot\nsudo apt install certbot\n\n# Obtain SSL certificate\nsudo certbot certonly --standalone -d your-domain.com\n\n# Update docker-compose.yml with certificate paths\n```\n\n#### Configure Backup\n\n```bash\n# Create backup directory\nsudo mkdir -p /backup/itechsmart\n\n# Set up automated backups\nsudo crontab -e\n\n# Add backup job (daily at 2 AM)\n0 2 * * * /opt/itechsmart/scripts/backup.sh\n```\n\n#### Configure Monitoring\n\n```bash\n# Enable monitoring\ndocker-compose -f docker-compose.yml -f docker-compose.monitoring.yml up -d\n\n# Access Grafana\n# http://your-domain.com:3000\n```\n\n---\n\n<a name="getting-started"></a>\n## 7. Getting Started\n\n### Initial Setup Wizard\n\nWhen you first access the iTechSmart Suite, you\'ll be guided through a setup wizard:\n\n#### Step 1: Administrator Account\n\nCreate your primary administrator account:\n- **Email:** Your email address\n- **Password:** Strong password (min 12 characters)\n- **Name:** Your full name\n- **Organization:** Your organization name\n\n#### Step 2: Organization Settings\n\nConfigure your organization:\n- **Organization Name:** Legal entity name\n- **Industry:** Healthcare, Finance, Technology, etc.\n- **Size:** Number of employees\n- **Location:** Primary location\n- **Timezone:** Your timezone\n\n#### Step 3: Product Selection\n\nChoose which products to enable:\n- ‚úÖ Select all products (recommended)\n- Or choose specific products for your needs\n\n#### Step 4: Integration Configuration\n\nConfigure integrations:\n- **Email Server:** SMTP settings for notifications\n- **Storage:** S3, Azure Blob, or local storage\n- **Authentication:** SSO, LDAP, or local auth\n\n#### Step 5: Security Settings\n\nConfigure security:\n- **Two-Factor Authentication:** Enable/disable\n- **Password Policy:** Complexity requirements\n- **Session Timeout:** Inactivity timeout\n- **IP Whitelist:** Restrict access by IP\n\n### Accessing Products\n\n#### Enterprise Hub (Central Dashboard)\n\n**URL:** `https://your-domain.com:3001`\n\nThe Enterprise Hub is your central control panel:\n- **Dashboard:** Overview of all products\n- **Product Launcher:** Quick access to all 33 products\n- **System Status:** Health monitoring\n- **User Management:** Manage users and permissions\n- **Settings:** System-wide configuration\n\n#### Individual Products\n\nEach product has its own interface:\n\n**Format:** `https://your-domain.com:30XX`\n\nWhere XX is the product number (01-33)\n\n**Examples:**\n- Ninja (AI Agent): `https://your-domain.com:3002`\n- Analytics: `https://your-domain.com:3003`\n- Supreme (Healthcare): `https://your-domain.com:3004`\n\n### User Management\n\n#### Creating Users\n\n1. Log in to Enterprise Hub\n2. Navigate to **Users** ‚Üí **Add User**\n3. Enter user details:\n   - Email address\n   - Name\n   - Role (Admin, User, Viewer)\n   - Product access permissions\n4. Click **Create User**\n5. User receives welcome email with login instructions\n\n#### Roles and Permissions\n\n**Administrator:**\n- Full access to all products\n- User management\n- System configuration\n- Billing and subscription\n\n**User:**\n- Access to assigned products\n- Create and edit content\n- View reports\n- Limited settings access\n\n**Viewer:**\n- Read-only access\n- View dashboards and reports\n- No editing capabilities\n\n#### Single Sign-On (SSO)\n\nConfigure SSO for seamless access:\n\n1. Navigate to **Settings** ‚Üí **Authentication**\n2. Select SSO provider (SAML, OAuth, LDAP)\n3. Enter provider details\n4. Test connection\n5. Enable SSO\n\n### Basic Operations\n\n#### Creating Your First Project\n\n1. Log in to Enterprise Hub\n2. Click **New Project**\n3. Enter project details:\n   - Project name\n   - Description\n   - Team members\n   - Products to use\n4. Click **Create**\n5. Start working!\n\n#### Inviting Team Members\n\n1. Navigate to **Team** ‚Üí **Invite Members**\n2. Enter email addresses (comma-separated)\n3. Select role and permissions\n4. Click **Send Invitations**\n5. Team members receive email invitations\n\n#### Configuring Notifications\n\n1. Navigate to **Settings** ‚Üí **Notifications**\n2. Choose notification channels:\n   - Email\n   - SMS\n   - Slack\n   - Microsoft Teams\n3. Set notification preferences\n4. Save settings\n\n---\n\n<a name="product-descriptions"></a>\n## 8. Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues and Solutions\n\n#### Issue: Cannot Access Web Interface\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Browser shows "Connection refused"\n- Timeout errors\n- SSL certificate errors\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check if services are running:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose ps\n   ```\n\n2. Verify ports are not blocked:\n   ```bash\n   sudo netstat -tulpn | grep 3001\n   ```\n\n3. Check firewall rules:\n   ```bash\n   sudo ufw status\n   ```\n\n4. Review logs:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose logs enterprise-frontend\n   ```\n\n5. Restart services:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose restart\n   ```\n\n---\n\n#### Issue: Database Connection Failed\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- "Database connection error"\n- Services fail to start\n- Timeout connecting to database\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check database status:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose ps postgres\n   ```\n\n2. Verify database credentials in `.env`\n\n3. Test database connection:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose exec postgres psql -U itechsmart -d itechsmart\n   ```\n\n4. Check database logs:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose logs postgres\n   ```\n\n5. Restart database:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose restart postgres\n   ```\n\n---\n\n#### Issue: High Memory Usage\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- System slowdown\n- Out of memory errors\n- Services crashing\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check memory usage:\n   ```bash\n   docker stats\n   ```\n\n2. Identify memory-hungry containers:\n   ```bash\n   docker stats --no-stream --format "table {{.Container}}\\t{{.MemUsage}}"\n   ```\n\n3. Increase memory limits in `docker-compose.yml`\n\n4. Restart services:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose restart\n   ```\n\n5. Consider upgrading server RAM\n\n---\n\n#### Issue: Slow Performance\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Slow page loads\n- Timeout errors\n- High response times\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check system resources:\n   ```bash\n   htop\n   ```\n\n2. Optimize database:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose exec postgres psql -U itechsmart -c "VACUUM ANALYZE;"\n   ```\n\n3. Clear cache:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose exec redis redis-cli FLUSHALL\n   ```\n\n4. Review logs for errors:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose logs --tail=100\n   ```\n\n5. Scale resources or add servers\n\n---\n\n#### Issue: SSL Certificate Errors\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- "Your connection is not private"\n- Certificate expired warnings\n- SSL handshake failures\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check certificate expiration:\n   ```bash\n   openssl x509 -in /path/to/cert.pem -noout -dates\n   ```\n\n2. Renew certificate:\n   ```bash\n   sudo certbot renew\n   ```\n\n3. Update certificate paths in configuration\n\n4. Restart web servers:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose restart\n   ```\n\n---\n\n#### Issue: Login Problems\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Cannot log in\n- "Invalid credentials" errors\n- Account locked\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Reset password via email\n\n2. Check user account status in database\n\n3. Clear browser cache and cookies\n\n4. Try different browser\n\n5. Contact administrator for account unlock\n\n---\n\n#### Issue: Services Not Starting\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Docker containers exit immediately\n- "Container exited with code 1"\n- Services in "Restarting" state\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check logs:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose logs [service-name]\n   ```\n\n2. Verify configuration files\n\n3. Check disk space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h\n   ```\n\n4. Verify environment variables in `.env`\n\n5. Remove and recreate containers:\n   ```bash\n   docker-compose down\n   docker-compose up -d\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Getting Help\n\nIf you cannot resolve an issue:\n\n1. **Check Documentation:** https://docs.itechsmart.ai\n2. **Search Community Forum:** https://community.itechsmart.ai\n3. **Contact Support:** support@itechsmart.ai\n4. **Emergency Support:** +1 (800) 911-TECH\n\nWhen contacting support, provide:\n- Product version\n- Error messages\n- Log files\n- Steps to reproduce\n- System information\n\n---\n\n<a name="warranty"></a>\n## 12. linux, windows, network_device\n    os_version = Column(String(100))\n    \n    # Connection details\n    ssh_port = Column(Integer, default=22)\n    winrm_port = Column(Integer, default=5985)\n    protocol = Column(Enum(CommandProtocol), default=CommandProtocol.SSH)\n    \n    # Credentials (encrypted)\n    credential_id = Column(String(36), ForeignKey(\'credentials.id\'))\n    \n    # Monitoring\n    prometheus_endpoint = Column(String(500))\n    wazuh_agent_id = Column(String(100))\n    \n    # Status\n    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)\n    last_seen = Column(DateTime)\n    health_status = Column(String(50))  # healthy, degraded, critical, offline\n    \n    # Metadata\n    tags = Column(JSON)\n    metadata = Column(JSON)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)\n    \n    # Relationships\n    credential = relationship("Credential", back_populates="servers")\n    incidents = relationship("Incident", back_populates="server")\n    metrics = relationship("ServerMetric", back_populates="server")\n    commands = relationship("CommandExecution", back_populates="server")\n\n\nclass Credential(Base):\n    """Secure credential storage"""\n    __tablename__ = "credentials"\n    \n    id = Column(String(36), primary_key=True)\n    name = Column(String(255), nullable=False)\n    credential_type = Column(String(50))  # ssh_key, password, api_token\n    \n    # Encrypted credentials\n    username = Column(String(255))\n    encrypted_password = Column(Text)\n    encrypted_private_key = Column(Text)\n    encrypted_api_token = Column(Text)\n    \n    # Vault reference\n    vault_path = Column(String(500))\n    \n    # Metadata\n    description = Column(Text)\n    tags = Column(JSON)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)\n    \n    # Relationships\n    servers = relationship("Server", back_populates="credential")\n\n\nclass Incident(Base):\n    """Infrastructure incident/issue"""\n    __tablename__ = "incidents"\n    \n    id = Column(String(36), primary_key=True)\n    title = Column(String(500), nullable=False)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    \n    # Classification\n    incident_type = Column(String(100))  # high_cpu, disk_full, service_down, security_breach, etc.\n    severity = Column(Enum(SeverityLevel), default=SeverityLevel.MEDIUM)\n    status = Column(Enum(IncidentStatus), default=IncidentStatus.DETECTED)\n    \n    #
